admin.constructionPlansPlacementDescription;Building Plans are placed on two rings around (0|0), with a predefined count on each ring.<br>Calculation:<br>At the start radius of rings are constant. Building Plans are placed equally on each ring, with one degree offset from zero degrees. <br>Then preliminary XY coordinates are calculated from degrees and radius. Next these coordinates are scaled to place the rings within the zone habited by players. <br>Scaling factor is calculated by distance from (0|0) where a new player would be placed. Then minimum distance is added, and then divided by a quotient.

anmelden.begruessung3_titel;Useful tips & information
anmelden.begruessung3;<b>As of {{WORLD_START_DATE}} at {{WORLD_START_TIME}}</b> Romans, Gauls and Teutons have begun struggling for dominance on this game world. Right now, <b>{{INT_SPIELER}} players in {{INT_ALLYS}} alliances</b> are fighting for supremacy. To not get lost in this devastating battle, you should look for allies even though you are protected by beginners protection for <b>{{INT_NOOB}} days</b>.<br><br>The Taskmaster will help you on your way to establishing your empire with advice, tasks and resources. He will reward you in different ways, after you manage to complete his tasks, such as finding out the exact duration of your beginner's protection.<br>You can find the Taskmaster on the left hand side of your village below your village name; he will be observing your progress while you take your first steps into Travian. Once you've successfully completed all of his tasks, you will be prepared to fend for yourself in this harsh world full of wars, battles and fellowships.<br><br>You will notice that you have started the game with a very special unit in your village - this unit is your Hero. The Hero is a very powerful soldier, and a powerful asset overall in the world of Travian. You can customize his appearance and create a Hero to represent you that best suits your liking. With your mighty Hero, you can lead your glorious armies to victory, conquer oasis's in the name of your empire and undertake dangerous and exciting adventures. <br>During his adventures, your Hero may find great treasures – he can discover long lost soldiers, capture wild animals or even find rare items of incredible power, which can later be equipped by your Hero to give him special bonuses and boosts. <br>But do not fret, for if your adventuring is unsuccessful, other players will often hold auctions where you can bid and buy items for your Hero; these auctions are performed via a special ingame currency called Silver. With Silver coins, you can participate in auctions and bid for some of the powerful items you require for your Hero.<br><br>You will notice that beside your fellow players, the world of Travian is also occupied by another tribe - the Natars, an ancient and legendary tribe of great power. Be careful when settling in their grey coloured area, for they will attack in order to defend their lands. The Natars are the only tribe that holds the secrets of constructing the fabled World Wonder, the greatest marvel of the Travian universe. They are a powerful force, so take heed when confronting them.<br><br><br>Keep in mind, though, that during your Travian experience, you have to heed the game rules<br>For further assistance with the game mechanics, more information concerning troops and buildings can be found in the game short instructions<br>If you're having problems and you are unsure how to continue the game, check out our Travian Answers first!<br>No solution? Try asking in the Forum<br>Tried everything to no avail? Write an answer to this message to contact the Support.<br><br><b>Travian game worlds run for roughly {{INT_LAUFZEIT}} months.</b> When you delete your account, or when a game world ends, you can move the remaining purchased Gold to another account, if applicable. Bear in mind, however, that Gold which has been converted to Silver cannot be transferred. The details will be explained to you in an email – you will receive this email immediately after you've terminated your account, or after the game world has ended. Keep in mind that the email will be sent to the email address the account has been registered to, so try not to lose or forget this address!<br>

anmelden.welcomeIGM_text_ROA;<b>As of {{WORLD_START_DATE}} at {{WORLD_START_TIME}}</b> Romans, Gauls and Teutons have begun struggling for dominance on this game world. Right now, <b>{{INT_SPIELER}} players in {{INT_ALLYS}} alliances</b> are fighting for supremacy. To not get lost in this devastating battle, you should look for allies even though you are protected by beginners protection for <b>{{INT_NOOB}} days</b>.<br><br>The Taskmaster will help you on your way to establishing your empire with advice, tasks and resources. He will reward you in different ways, after you manage to complete his tasks, such as finding out the exact duration of your beginner's protection.<br>You can find the Taskmaster on the left hand side of your village below your village name; he will be observing your progress while you take your first steps into Travian. Once you've successfully completed all of his tasks, you will be prepared to fend for yourself in this harsh world full of wars, battles and fellowships.<br><br>You will notice that you have started the game with a very special unit in your village - this unit is your Hero. The Hero is a very powerful soldier, and a powerful asset overall in the world of Travian. You can customize his appearance and create a Hero to represent you that best suits your liking. With your mighty Hero, you can lead your glorious armies to victory and conquer oases in the name of your empire. <br><br><br>Keep in mind, though, that during your Travian experience, you have to heed the game rules<br>For further assistance with the game mechanics, more information concerning troops and buildings can be found in the game short instructions<br>If you're having problems and you are unsure how to continue the game, check out our Travian Answers first!<br>No solution? Try asking in the Forum<br>Tried everything to no avail? Write an answer to this message to contact the Support.<br><br><b>Travian game worlds run for roughly {{INT_LAUFZEIT}} months.</b> When you delete your account, or when a game world ends, you can move the remaining purchased Gold to another account, if applicable. The details will be explained to you in an email – you will receive this email immediately after you've terminated your account, or after the game world has ended. Keep in mind that the email will be sent to the email address the account has been registered to, so try not to lose or forget this address!<br>

anmelden.welcomeIGM_text_AS2017;Welcome {{PLAYERNAME}},This is your new home.Take a look around. The lush fields, the golden crop and the iron mountains - they all belong to you. Your village may be small right now, but with enough wit and hard work, you will transform it into an empire. Still, a great ruler needs more than virtue – a great ruler needs wisdom. So hear me out:<br>The world revolves around resources. Your buildings need them, your troops eat them, and whole wars will be waged over nothing else. Yet, it’s important that you understand: Resources are a means to an end. Spend them, always. Your beginner’s protection will fade and raiders won’t wait long. Log in regularly and invest in the Cranny and more resource fields to keep a thriving economy.<br>Take a deep breath. The air may still be fresh from the rain, but there's a hint of ash. You cannot escape the signs of war. But the art of diplomacy needs no longer be a secret: Speak to others. Find friends and join an alliance. They will support you in times of need and provide you with countless advice. You should also write to your aggressors. You will find that a deal can often be made that benefits you both.<br>Now lay the first stone. This is your monument. But it won’t be the only one. Your plan should be to settle a second village as soon as you can. Your options and therefore your power will increase greatly. Plenty more resources, additional ways to specialize with buildings and hence better strategies. Settling closer to your friends is also a benefit that should not be ignored.<br>No more words should be wasted. It is time for action. Consult the Taskmaster – he has great plans for you already. Let me finish with one invaluable piece of wisdom: You have never truly lost until you have given up. There will be challenges and there will be setbacks, though only through overcoming those will you grow. Every great story involves some hardship. Now go out there and show the world what you are made of.

gid37.oase_verlassen;Abandon oasis
gid37.dauer;Duration
gid37.fertig;Finished
gid37.oasen_faq;What are oases? <br>There are tiles with forests, mountains, clay pits and croplands on the map. <br>These tiles can be occupied with a hero and offer the corresponding occupying village a resource production increase.<br><br>Currently you do not own any oases.<br><br><br>How do I occupy an oasis? <br>You can occupy oases by attacking an oasis repeatedly with a hero. The occupied oasis is added to the village from whitch the hero attacked. Remember that an oasis has to be within the radius of the small map area surrounding your village (centre your village!) to be conquerable.<br>You need a Hero's Mansion level 10, 15 or 20 to conquer an oasis.<br><br>You can only have 3 oases per village.<br> <br><br>Can one desert oases? <br>Yes, that is possible. After you occupied at least one oasis, this option will become available in your Hero's Mansion.<br><br>Occupying/attacking player-owned oases<br>To occupy an oasis owned by another player, you have to destroy the defence in the oasis and attack it with your hero several times. <br>Hint: Your hero will not vanish after occupying oases like administrators (Senator, Chief, Chieftain) do after conquering villages and will be continue to exist like before.<br><br>Raiding an oasis will cause your troops to also plunder the village owning the oasis; the attacked village will lose 10% of its resources per attack in 10 minutes.<br><br>Defending oases <br>In order to defend an oasis against raids, you can reinforce it with troops. To send them back, select the rally point of the village owning the oasis and withdraw them. Sending crop to an oasis to feed troops is not necessary, since the troops are fed directly from the village owning the oasis.<br>For more information about oases take a look at the Travian Answers.

manual.tid1;The Legionnaire is the simple and all-purpose infantry of the Roman Empire. With his well-rounded training, he is good at both defence and offence. However, the Legionnaire will never reach the levels of the more specialized troops.

manual.tid2;The Praetorians are the emperor's guard and they defend him with their life. Because their training is specialized for defence, they are very weak attackers.

manual.tid3;The Imperian is the ultimate attacker of the Roman Empire. He is quick, strong, and the nightmare of all defenders. However, his training is expensive and time-intensive.

manual.tid3Answers_title;Travian Answers
manual.tid4;The Equites Legati are the roman reconnaissance troops. They are pretty fast and can spy on enemy villages in order to see resources and troops.<br><br>If there are no Scouts, Equites Legati or Pathfinders in the scouted village, the scouting remains unnoticed.
manual.tid4Answers;153
manual.tid4Answers_title;Travian Answers
manual.tid5;The Equites Imperatoris are the standard cavalry of the roman army and are very well armed. They are not the fastest troops, but are a horror for unprepared enemies. You should, however, always keep in mind that catering for horse and rider isn't cheap.
manual.tid5Answers;154
manual.tid5Answers_title;Travian Answers
manual.tid6;The Equites Caesaris are the heavy cavalry of Rome. They are very well armored and deal great amounts of damage, but all that armor and weaponry comes with a price. They are slow, carry less resources and feeding them is expensive.

manual.tid7Answers_title;Travian Answers
manual.tid8;The Catapult is an excellent long-distance weapon; it is used to destroy the fields and buildings of enemy villages. However, without escorting troops, it is virtually defenseless, so don't forget to send some of your troops with it. <br><br>Having a high-level rally point makes your catapults more accurate and gives you the option to target additional enemy buildings. More information is available here.<br>HINT: Catapults CAN hit the cranny, trappers or stonemason's lodges when they target randomly.
manual.tid8Answers;157
manual.tid8Answers_title;Travian Answers
manual.tid9;The Senator is the tribe's chosen leader. He's a good speaker and knows how to convince others. He is able to persuade other villages to fight for your empire. <br><br>Every time the Senator speaks to the inhabitants of a village, the enemy's loyalty value decreases until the village is yours.
manual.tid9Answers;158

They need a basic supplies of 750 units per resource.
manual.tid10Answers;159

He moves on foot, which makes him slower than his Roman or Gaul counterparts. He scouts the enemy units, resources and fortifications. <br><br>If there are no enemy Scouts, Pathfinders or Equites Legati in the scouted village then the scouting remains unnoticed.

Their training takes very long and is rather expensive.

manual.gid18;The embassy is a place for diplomats. At level 1 you can join an alliance, and after extending it to level 3 you may even found one yourself. <br><br>The maximum number of possible members in an alliance is equal to 3 times the level of the highest level embassy within that alliance. Therefore, with a level 20 embassy, there can be up to 60 players in an alliance.

manual.eventstau;event jam (00:00:0?)
manual.eventstau_text;All events occurring at a later time get calculated by an event system. In case the server is overloaded or the connection between the web server and the database is slow, an event jam can occur.<br><br>If more events are received per second than can be calculated per second, events (e.g. "construction finished" or "troops arrived") will be put into a waiting loop.<br><br>The chronological order of troop movements stays the same, even in case of an event jam, so troops that would normally arrive somewhere first would still arrive there as planned.<br><br>As a player, nothing can be done against an event jam except for waiting it out. Normally, these problems get resolved after a few minutes automatically. At the moment, {{INT}} events are waiting to get calculated.
manual.top10_stats;Top 10 statistics
manual.top10_text1;The Top 10 statistics are recreated each week and are valid from Monday 00:00 until Sunday 24:00 GMT+1.
manual.top10_text2;At the end of each week, the top ten players are awarded a special decoration. When you edit your profile, a certain code (e.g. {{#123}}) is displayed at "medals" which can be inserted where desired. Examples:

manual.random_artefact_title;Artefact of the fool
manual.random_artefact_text;Wanting nothing more then glory and fame for himself, an ancient Natarian emperor order his finest craftsmen to construct magical items which would come to be known as artefacts.<br><br>Taking up this challenge, they began working on these powerful creations. But their first attempt could not have gone more horribly right. They created a powerful item capable of giving any power they could think of at the time of making it.<br><br>It only possessed one slight downside; although it could grant any bonus to its holder, it changed its power every 24h. For this reason, the crafters named it the Artefact of fools.

manual.v8;Spartans
manual.tid71;The Hoplites were the most common units of the Greek city states. With their universal training and attention to physical fitness, they are moderately good at attacking and can carry many resources. Hoplites also have an average defense, both against infantry and cavalry. Due to the need for comprehensive training, their training time is not the fastest.
manual.tid72;Sentinels dedicate their lives to searching for secrets other tribes might hide. They typically travel on foot and in disguise, which allows them to sneak into highly secured sanctuaries unnoticed. Just like all Spartans, they receive excellent training, which makes them not only tireless runners but also good defenders. In defense, Sentinels stand shoulder to shoulder with others and will fight to the death!
manual.tid73;Shieldsmen are elite defenders, the best the world has ever seen. They undergo high-level training starting from childhood. Due to their dedication, they can move extremely fast despite their heavy armor and enormous shields. As a result, they are excellent in battle against enemy infantry, creating unbreakable walls that are more robust than houses made of brick.
manual.tid74;Meet an absolute beast! These fearless and experienced attackers strike horror into the hearts of those who hear their war cry. Thanks to them having two blades, Twinsteel Therions can maintain the initiative indefinitely during an attack. They break through any defense just like a hot knife through butter. Their training may be expensive and take a lot of time, but they are worth it!
manual.tid75;Elpida means “hope,” which is precisely what these brave riders bring to villages under attack. Fast and relentless, they will rush to your aid while riding on their gracious horses. They are well-trained to resist both cavalry and infantry, and they are also the fastest units of the Spartan army. Unfortunately, their attack is relatively weak.
manual.tid76;Corinthian Crushers are an elite attacking cavalry in the Spartan army. As solid and disciplined riders in their bronze Corinthian helmets, they are a true legend. These units need space to show their worth. Therefore, they are better suited for attack than defense. They might not be the fastest riders, but when they arrive at the battle, their enemies tremble!
manual.tid77;The ram is a heavy support weapon for your infantry and cavalry. Its task is to destroy the enemy walls and increase your troops’ chances of overcoming the enemy's fortifications.
manual.tid78;Ballistae launch iron bolts with such force that they can crush any building in the blink of an eye. Do not send them alone though! Without reasonable assistance and left unprotected, Ballistae are especially vulnerable against cavalry attacks.
manual.tid79;Integrity and loyalty are the features that make Ephors great leaders. Strong yet not disrespectful, kind but not weak, they can persuade anyone to do what they believe is right.<br><br>Every time they step foot into an enemy village, their powerful presence reduces the people's loyalty to their owner until they decide to join your command.
manual.tid80;Settlers are brave and daring citizens who move out of the village, after a lot of training, to establish a new village in your honor.<br><br>As both the journey and the founding of the new village are very difficult, three settlers must stick together. They need basic supplies of 750 units per resource.

plus.ig_goldclub_nightwatch_title;Night watch
plus.ig_goldclub_nightwatch;The night watch contains of troops from your tribe. The bigger your village, the more troops will be send. The night watch will protect your village for {{INT}} nights, exept they get destroyed or are send away. The troops will deliver crop for 10 hours worth of their supply. If your Granary is not large enough or you send the crop for other things, the night watch may starve. The night watch needs 2 hours to arrive. If you call the night watch during the night, they still need 2 hours to arrive and will only be send if the night lasts for at least 2 hours. Otherwise the night watch will arrive during the next night. The night watch will leave your village after 10 hours and will return during the next night.

sysmsg.gameplay_phase2_name;Midgame artefacts
sysmsg.gameplay_phase2_text;Artefacts<br><br>Whispered rumors echo through the villages, containing legends told only by the best of storytellers. They concern the Natars, Travian’s most fearsome warriors. It is every hero’s dream to slay them, every soldier’s goal. No one knows how the Natars grew to be so powerful, their soldiers so fearsome. Determined to discover the source of their power, an elite group of scouts is sent out to spy.  They return a few hours later with terrified faces and wild theories: it seems the Natars’ power comes from mysterious items they call artefacts, which they had stolen from your ancestors. Manage to steal the artefacts, they say, and you can steal their power.<br><br><br><br>The time has come to reclaim the artefacts. Conspire with your alliance and assemble your warriors to retrieve these coveted objects. However, the Natars will not give the artefacts up without a fight… and neither shall your enemies. If you can manage to successfully repossess the artefacts and fend off your enemies, then you will be able to reap the rewards. Your buildings shall become incredibly strong and powerful, your troops much faster and more crop-efficient. Seize the artefacts, bring glory to your empire, and become the new legends for your successors.<br><br><br>(Story by Cryptid_Hunter)<br><br> <br><br>» continue<br><br>
sysmsg.gameplay_phase3_name;Wonder of the World
sysmsg.gameplay_phase3_text;Wonders Of The World<br><br>Days fade into nights that seem ever longer as the cruel chills of winter begin their descent upon a people weary of war. <br>The first snowflakes dance across the night sky, foretelling the end of all that was and all that will be.<br><br><br>The glorious victories of the past no longer seem as wonderful in the latest retelling. <br>They are but memories of a time when men felt immortal. <br>The old warriors huddle beside the fire and remember fondly the great friends they had fought beside and lost, now but distant shadows in the darkness. <br>The armies and triumphs of the past have lost their lustre, and those still left standing wonder what they continue to fight for and whether there is anything worth still fighting for. <br>They resolve that they will not go so silently into the winter night, that this age, their age, will be one to be remembered.<br><br>They pledged to search across the world for knowledge of the wonders of the past, hidden in history, in a world that is now legend, in a world that is beyond memory. <br>Heroes and armies searched far and wide across the fields, forests and mountains, braving the elements and their enemies to bring the secrets of the lost past back home. <br>After many bitter disappointments a muse smiled upon some unknown hero and guided him to the revelation that a tribe of that long lost past yet lurked among the living ---- The Dreaded Natars. <br>The Natars are steeped in lore and mystery, an ancient race so feared for their savagery in battle that they are told as bedtime stories to scare children.<br><br>With much trepidation, the armies of Travian bid farewell to their loved ones, possibly for the last time, to march into the villages of the Natarian Empire. <br>Hundreds of thousands of souls marched on the crowded roads beneath a winter sky to their destiny. <br>There was no fear in their eyes, no hesitation, for they knew it was their chance, their only chance, to leave this age with not a whisper, but a roar, a declaration, that they existed. <br>A declaration that will last throughout the ages, to become story, song and legend.<br><br>Beneath the winter sky, the flickering lights of the Natarian villages waited for the hundreds of armies marching towards them, the Dread Armies of the Dead Empire prepared to defend the valuable points from which they had once controlled the world, knowing that the many advantages that lay within each would be crucial to the fate of the world and its many peoples. <br><br>(Story by Grozoth)<br>» continue
sysmsg.gameplay_phase4_name;Construction plans
sysmsg.gameplay_phase4_text;Construction plans<br><br>Countless days have passed since the first battles upon the walls of the cursed villages of the dreaded Natars, many armies of both the free ones and the Natarian empire struggled and died before the walls of the many strongholds from which the Natars had once ruled all creation. <br>Now with the dust settled and as a tentative sense of calm spread among the remaining soldiers, armies began to count their losses and collect their dead, the stench of combat still lingering in the night air, a smell of a slaughter unforgettable in its extent and brutality soon to be dwarfed by yet others. <br>The largest armies of the free tribes were preparing for another attack, and the fearsome Natars were marshalling their defences for yet another renewed assault upon the coveted former strongholds of the Natarian Empire. <br><br>Soon, scouts arrived with tales of a most awesome sight and a chilling reminder; a dreaded army of an unfathomable size had been spotted treading its path towards the very end of the world, the Natarian capital, a force so great that the dust from their march would choke off all light, a force so brutal and ruthless that it would crush all hope. <br>The free people knew thay they had to do the impossible; race against time and the endless hordes of the Natarian Empire to raise a Wonder of the World in order to restore peace to the world and vanquish the Natarian threat once and for all.<br><br>But to raise such a great Wonder would be no easy task; one would need construction plans created and long forgotten in the distant past, plans of such an arcane nature that even the very wisest of sages knew not their contents or locations. <br><br>Tens of thousands of scouts roamed across all existence searching in vain for these mystical plans, looking in all places but the dreaded Natarian Capital, yet could not find them. <br>Today however, they return baring good news; the locations of the plans have finally been discovered, concealed by the armies of the Natars inside secret strongholds, purposefully constructed to be hidden from the eyes of man.<br><br>Now begins the final stretch, when the greatest armies of the free peoples and the Natars will clash upon the largest battlefields of the world to decide the fate of all that lies under heaven. <br>Sword against sword, this is the war that will echo across the eons; this is your war, and here you shall etch your name across history. <br>Here you shall become legend...<br><br>(Story by Grozoth)<br><br><br><br><b>Facts:</b>To steal one, the following things must happen:<br><br>    You must attack the village (NO Raid!)<br>    WIN the Attack<br>    Destroy the treasury<br>    Hero must participate in an attack<br>    An empty treasury level 10 MUST be in the village where that attack came from<br><br><br>If not, the next attack on that village, winning with a hero and empty treasury will take the building plan.<br><br>To build a WW from level 0 to 49, you must own an active construction plan (you = the WW village owner.<br>To build a WW from level 50 to 100, you must own an active construction plan (you = the WW village owner) AND someone else in your alliance must own an active construction plan. Confederacy does not count! Builder owning two plans does not work, they only count as one!<br>» continue

sysmsg.natar_start_text;Natars are starting to build their Wonder of the World<br><br>A long time ago the Natars were feared soldiers. They dominated the Travian world and nobody dared to oppose them. They build the Wonder of the World and kept all the artefacts. What was keeping them so strong was their Emperor, whom they considered a god. Everybody feared him. Some Natars liked him, some didn’t. Of course they would never admit, for who said as much as a word against him would be killed. He was formidable; he inspired his soldiers. One day however, the Emperor disappeared. Nobody knew what happened to him. Many people didn’t believe it, either because they didn’t want to believe it or they thought it’s a trick to get them to finally talk against him and be killed. But months passed and the Emperor didn’t return. And as much as the new Natarian council of leaders tried to inspire their soldiers, it didn’t work. They tried to keep the missing of the Emperor a secret, but soon all the other tribes knew as well. They saw this as their chance and started attacking all the artefact villages. They stole one after another and when they were done, they started stealing WW plans. The Natars lost most plans and stopped building WW. And from then on the Natars didn’t build a single WW. However, everything is about to change! News came that the Emperor is back! And he is angrier than ever! Not much is known, but it is sure that now the Natars started building their Wonder of the World! Do you dare to attack them, now that the Emperor is back?<br><br>(Story by Filip)<br><br><br><br>» continue

sysmsg.constructionPlansAnnouncement_title;Construction plans have spawned
sysmsg.constructionPlansAnnouncement_quote;"An ungodly stench of copper filled the air. The Natarian empire was discovered, and this called for force. Bones cracked and crunched as a horde of Natarian beasts smashed into the front lines. Sounds of metal on metal were heard clinking and clashing under a blood moon sky. We discovered the exact location of ancient construction plans for this Wonder of the World and, should we fulfill these plans, the Natars would fall. Now, it was a race against time. We had to be the first to build this Wonder of the World among all the chaos. No other alliance could do so before us! It was time to decide our fate."
